We brought in our 1986 Toyota RV for a smog and emissions test. The RV failed twice but Lathrop Smog did not fail us. We would highly recommend them in you are in the area.< /review>

< review>
I normally love going to this location. The employees are always super friendly when I walk in. The pizza is delicious and their bread has it's days on being fresh or being hard. Well, last night I went and got a pizza and when I got home I noticed that it was burnt and extra thin. I ordered the normal $5 pizza. So I was a little bummed because I've never had an issue. I tried to eat a slice, and I couldn't.  It was just rock hard from being burnt or in their hot box too long. It honestly tasted like cardboard. I just called and spoke to their manager and all he could say was sorry about that what do you want me to do? First of all as a manager that is not how you handle the situation, and secondly there was no reason to be rude about it. I will not be returning to this location again. Make sure you check your pizza before leaving the location just so you dont get stuck with a burnt pizza or ask for a fresh one to be made!!</review>

They rented the vehicle out to someone else. Was told because I did not show up on time, I lost my reservation. Was told I can go and contact other places on my own.
I was very calm and reserved but firm.

One staff member was a complete jerk.
Was rolling his eyes and started engaging in a verbal altercation with me.
How unprofessional.
Expedia does not list that reservation is forfeited if you don't show up on time.
I booked hundreds of vehicles before and never ran into this problem. Things come up and flights get delayed. I called and told expedia they need to add a warning on their booking page so people are aware.</Text>
